** If you define CENs, Service Providers, and Subscribers, there is another layer of tests
  Look for the SLS configuration below and the automated Must Statement tests that match to all the [R#] requirements are at the very bottom.
****


====================>Start with the Minimal Complexity User Interface Tests

$ ncs_cli -u admin -C 

admin connected from 127.0.0.1 using console on mylo
admin@ncs# source init_MEF_Tests_Minimal.txt
